Visual Issues (10)
warning overflow: div.fixed
What: The element div.fixed extends beyond the viewport width.
Why: This causes horizontal scrolling on this device, making the page feel broken. Common causes: fixed-width elements, images without max-width, or padding/margin pushing content out.
Fix: Add overflow-x: hidden to the container, or use max-width: 100% on the overflowing element. Check if a parent has explicit width wider than the viewport.

Why: This causes horizontal scrolling on this device, making the page feel broken. Common causes: fixed-width elements, images without max-width, or padding/margin pushing content out.
Fix: Add overflow-x: hidden to the container, or use max-width: 100% on the overflowing element. Check if a parent has explicit width wider than the viewport.

Visual Issues (10)
warning overflow: div.fixed
What: The element div.fixed extends beyond the viewport width.
Why: This causes horizontal scrolling on this device, making the page feel broken. Common causes: fixed-width elements, images without max-width, or padding/margin pushing content out.
Fix: Add overflow-x: hidden to the container, or use max-width: 100% on the overflowing element. Check if a parent has explicit width wider than the viewport.

HTML: <h4 class="mb-1 text-xs font-bold text-white svelte-jz8lnl">Company HQ</h4>
Why this matters: This degrades the experience for users with disabilities and may violate WCAG 2.1 AA compliance requirements.
Learn more: https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/heading-order?application=playwright

warning overflow: div.fixed
What: The element div.fixed extends beyond the viewport width.
Why: This causes horizontal scrolling on this device, making the page feel broken. Common causes: fixed-width elements, images without max-width, or padding/margin pushing content out.
Fix: Add overflow-x: hidden to the container, or use max-width: 100% on the overflowing element. Check if a parent has explicit width wider than the viewport.

What: Ensure buttons have discernible text

Visual Issues (10)
warning overflow: div.fixed
What: The element div.fixed extends beyond the viewport width.
Why: This causes horizontal scrolling on this device, making the page feel broken. Common causes: fixed-width elements, images without max-width, or padding/margin pushing content out.
Fix: Add overflow-x: hidden to the container, or use max-width: 100% on the overflowing element. Check if a parent has explicit width wider than the viewport.
